discoveri OF gold IN california john S hittel


befor time great gold discoveri metal
found california mine taken poor
yield small return year work the discoveri
influenc whole world give new life trade industri

the coup detat OF loui napoleon alexi de tocquevil


By astound act decemb known coup detat
charl loui napoleon bonapart commonli call loui napoleon
practic assum imperi power first anniversari
coup detat offici proclaim emperor french
titl napoleon He son loui bonapart king
holland brother napoleon born pari april
